The selection you make for 'Purpose' determines if you need to specify a 'Sales Opportunity number' and the 'reservation policy' (how long the environment is available and how often it can be extended).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEnsure that you keep the default selection '\u003cstrong\u003eall\u003c/strong\u003e' in the 'Starter Service' dropdown.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\techzone-reservation_2301.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\techzone-reservation_2301.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eOnce you have reserved an environment in IBM TechZone, it is first \u003cstrong\u003eScheduled\u003c/strong\u003e for provisioning. After a while it moves into status \u003cstrong\u003eProvisioning\u003c/strong\u003e, and after some time it finally becomes \u003cstrong\u003eReady\u003c/strong\u003e. Overall this may take up to 6 hours. You will receive several emails during that period.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe final email has the subject '\u003cstrong\u003eReservation Ready on IBM Technology Zone\u003c/strong\u003e'. It contains a link '\u003cstrong\u003eView My Reservations\u003c/strong\u003e' to get to your reservations. Click on this link and click on the tile that represents your reservation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\your-environment-is-ready_2301.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\your-environment-is-ready_2301.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAt the bottom of the screen for your environment, you'll find the \u003cstrong\u003ePakInstaller Portal URL\u003c/strong\u003e that you require.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\techzone-reserved-env_2301.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\techzone-reserved-env_2301.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGetting access to the OpenShift Web Console (optional)\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eOpen the PakInstaller Portal using the link shown on the reservation details page in IBM TechZone. On the \u003cstrong\u003eOpenShift Console\u003c/strong\u003e tab of the PakInstaller Portal, you'll find the link to the \u003cstrong\u003eOpenShift Web Console\u003c/strong\u003e together with the \u003cstrong\u003eadmin user\u003c/strong\u003e (always ocpadmin) and the \u003cstrong\u003epassword\u003c/strong\u003e (unique to each provisioned environment).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\pakinstaller-portal_2301.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\pakinstaller-portal_2301.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can use the OpenShift Web Console to validate that the Cloud Pak is fully installed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen logging into the OpenShift Web Console make sure to select \u003cstrong\u003eDaffy htpasswd Provider\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\openshift-login-selection.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\openshift-login-selection.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEnvironment Validation\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAfter the final email, it may still take some time until the Cloud Pak is fully operational. \u003cstrong\u003ePeriodically check until your environment is ready\u003c/strong\u003e. For this, perform the following steps:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOpen the \u003cstrong\u003eOpenShift Web Console\u003c/strong\u003e (see above) in a browser\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClick on \u003cstrong\u003eWorkloads -\u0026gt; ConfigMaps\u003c/strong\u003e in the left-hand side navigator\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eType '\u003cstrong\u003eaccess-info\u003c/strong\u003e' in the field next to 'Name'\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf the ConfigMap '\u003cstrong\u003eicp4adeploy-cp4ba-access-info\u003c/strong\u003e' is shown, your CP4BA cluster is fully deployed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eb) Everybody else\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eCreate or use a CP4BA 23.2.2 Starter deployment authoring environment with at least the following capabilities: Business Applications, Automation Decision Services, Workflow, Business Automation Insights, and optionally Automation Document Processing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMachine to start deployment from\u003c/strong\u003e\nA Windows, Linux, or Mac system with \u003cstrong\u003eJava 8\u003c/strong\u003e or later installed is required to start the deployment of the Client Onboarding artifacts. You can execute it multiple times without causing any issues. It will skip over those deployment steps that have already been successfully performed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSometimes the deployment fails because of timing or network issues. These may not occur again when triggering the deployment a second time.\u003c/strong\u003e Other failures have been observed where the CP4BA environment or some of its PODs had issues and needed to be restarted.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor the purpose of analyzing issues the deployment tool creates four files in the directory where it is located:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003edeployClientOnboarding_23.2.2_Starter_output.txt - Contains the messages printed to the console\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003edeployClientOnboarding_23.2.2_Starter_detailedOutput.txt - Everything printed to the console plus details about the deployment steps\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003edeployClientOnboarding_23.2.2_Starter_trace.txt - Contains very detailed trace messages about everthing that is done as part of running a deployment\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003edeployClientOnboarding_23.2.2_Starter_combined.txt - Contains a combination of the detailedOutput and trace files\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp V4.x\u003c/strong\u003e \u003c/a\u003e (make sure to use \u003cstrong\u003eV4.x\u003c/strong\u003e). Wait until you receive an email from IBM TechZone with the title \"Reservation Ready on IBM Technology Zone\".\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eOnce the environment is ready, select open your reservation on the IBM TechZone 'My Reservations' page. At the bottom of the screen you find a large blue button below the header 'VM Remote Console'. It will bring up the Windows desktop as part of the browser window. \u003cstrong\u003eThis is the recommended way to connect to the RPA VM for demoing the bot execution.\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\rpa-vm-browser-rdp.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\rpa-vm-browser-rdp.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePrior to testing/demoing:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/em\u003e Start Firefox, the browser used by the bot, once and ensure that no update or similar is pending. This could interfere with executing the bot. Afterwards close the browser again.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConfiguration\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou need to set the following two variables in the bat/sh-file you downloaded and edited previously:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003erpaBotExecutionUser\u003c/code\u003e - Set to the user for who the RPA bot should be executed for (would normally be \u003ccode\u003ecp4admin\u003c/code\u003e). Setting it to a non-existing user like cp4admin2 will always skip the actual bot invocation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003erpaServer\u003c/code\u003e - Set this to the URL of the RPA environment that you provisioned as described above. Use the URL listed as \u003ccode\u003eRPA Asynch Server API\u003c/code\u003e at the top of your reservation on IBM TechZone.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/blob/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\rpa-reservation-async-url.jpg\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/IBM/cp4ba-client-onboarding-scenario/raw/main/23.2.2/..\\images\\rpa-reservation-async-url.jpg\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you have previously run the deployment, run it again. It will recognize that your RPA configuration has changed and will redeploy the artifact that contains the changed RPA information.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\"
